Because it was Qingming Festival, the weather was not very sunny, and the photos were a bit gloomy, but I was amazed by it since I entered the hotel group. The hotel is surrounded by mountains and rivers, birds and flowers, and it just rained heavily in the morning. The temperature is moderate and the air is particularly fresh. The hotel service is online throughout the whole process. The front desk lady introduced the package in detail. The room was ready very early, and a box of fireworks was given to the children. Butler Yao Yao added WeChat to provide caring service around the clock. When he encountered heavy rain in the aquarium, he tracked the whole process and sent a car to deliver an umbrella. He returned to the hotel to deliver ginger tea. He was meticulous in all aspects. I booked a two-bedroom villa, which is very large and clean, with a wide view and a very OK scenery. The room is a duplex, with a tea room, microwave and refrigerator, and the bathroom uses L'Occitane, and drinks are free. There is a battery car to pick up and drop off at any time to the room. Breakfast is on the first floor of the hotel, but the buffet and heated swimming pool are in the hotel next door (Shiboge), which also has a battery car to pick up and drop off at any time. The hotel is great overall. Although I missed the sunshine these few days, staying here can make people feel relaxed and happy. It is great to rest and vacation üëç

name:V‚ÄçV‚Äçy‚Äçu‚Äçn‚Äçy‚Äçu‚Äçn
info:Deluxe Villa - 2-Bedroom, Courtyard-View
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:4 Reviews
rating:4.5
posted:Posted May 7, 2024
msg:Someone asked me why I write reviews so seriously? Every time I travel, I always encounter various situations. It is not only a good memory, but also a practical sharing, which may help you who are still choosing, or you who are hesitating, or the business that needs improvement.
Overall, it is wise to choose Songpin during the May Day holiday. The hotel area is large and the facilities are complete. Even if you do not leave the hotel, it is enough to play for 2-3 days.
Transportation: It is a certain distance from the high-speed rail station, and it is more convenient to drive there. There are multiple parking lots with ample parking spaces. There are battery cars in the hotel for pick-up. You have to wait for about 10 minutes during peak hours, but it is still quite fast at other times.
Environment: The hotel was originally owned by Wanda. It was acquired by Sunac around 18 and 19, and a hotel group and amusement park were developed. It has a large area and an artificial lake. The distant view is the typical karst mountain scenery of Guilin. Although it is not as beautiful as the Ten-mile Gallery in Yangshuo, it also has certain characteristics. The hotel group is divided into Shiboge and Songpin. Songpin has more than 90 different villas in Chinese style, which are quite distinctive.
Service: From the beginning of check-in, it is generally thoughtful and convenient. The front desk staff actively added WeChat, provided butler-style service, and answered questions, guided, and booked cars in a timely manner. The hotel supplies are also very generous. A box of bottled water was directly brought to the room to ensure a box of water per day. Disadvantages: The service details need to be benchmarked against the international five-star level, such as the time for booking bamboo rafts by phone, which was wrong twice. Some waiters are not familiar with the surrounding roads, etc.
Facilities: In terms of room supplies, the most complained thing is the disposable slippers, all of which are size 43, regardless of gender, or children's. It is very unfriendly to girls, and this aspect can be completely improved. Other supplies are basically complete and tasteful.
Dining: Songpin Buffet Restaurant is in Huli, with good scenery. Unfortunately, it only opens breakfast during the May Day holiday, and dinner is arranged at Shiboge. Although there are battery cars to pick up and drop off, there are more people, and the products are also average (basically frozen ingredients), and the experience is not very good.
Entertainment: Since the package was ordered, 4 bamboo rafts and tickets to two parks have been included. Bamboo rafts need to be booked one day in advance. In fact, they are electric boats that can seat about 10 people. It is a good experience to browse on the artificial lake for 20 minutes when the weather is good. As for the evaluation of the two Sunac Parks: Sea World is better than expected, there are more animals than expected, and there are many feeding projects (although the price is expensive); Happy World is suitable for children, and it is not very attractive to adults. Many restaurants and stores around are closed, so it is not very popular. The popularity during the May Day holiday is average, and I hope it will get better and better.
Travel photography: The Platinum Travel Photography I gave away feels so-so. Maybe the merchant saw that we didn't put on makeup or change into designated clothes, so they sent us a temporary photographer. I am not familiar with the hotel enough, and the experience is not very good. But I understand the difficulty of the May Day peak season, so I didn't complain and bought all the few photos. I hope I will do it more attentively in the future.

The two hotels are actually across the lake. The design of the lake surface and the design of the hotel garden are completely integrated with mountains and water. The lake is sparkling, comparable to Lugu Lake in Yunnan!
The car drove to the entrance of the Mandarin Hotel, and a tall and thin concierge came over to help us open the door. His smile made me feel more cordial, and he was very attentive to help me unload my luggage, and then guide me to the front hall of the hotel. , assist us to scan the code to measure the temperature, the epidemic prevention work is very in place, the little sister in national costume is really beautiful, she greeted us with a sweet voice, although she wears a mask, but she can feel her is very enthusiastic. The environment of the whole hotel is a very elegant and generous Chinese style, with a strong cultural heritage. The check-in procedure was very fast. The lady at the front desk politely asked me about my personal preferences. After the check-in procedure, she also gave me a large basket of fruits, which was so happy and unexpected!
Since it is a single-family villa, it is necessary to take a battery car for a while from the check-in procedure to the arrival of the room. The little brother who drove the hotel introduced us to the hotel and the surrounding facilities. You can also go kayaking at the second pier. , If you don't dare to row a boat, you can make an appoin**ent for a bamboo raft. There is a special person responsible for opening the bamboo raft, and then you can sit on it and pat it all. The experience is very good.
The single-family villa is really comfortable, the bedding is very good, the bed is very comfortable, and taking a bath in the villa is just one word: cool! Because of the showers, the air is very fresh after the rain, and it is completely immersed in nature. The room is really big, there is a separate courtyard, you can stare at the lake view, you can sit quietly and listen to the birds.
The breakfast is also very delicious. It is in the form of a set menu. It is so exquisite. It is really worth spending this money to stay at the Mandarin Hotel for one night.
After breakfast, I walked around the hotel quietly. The waiters at the hotel would greet us, especially able to chat. They could chat with us for half an hour without repetition, which made us feel very friendly and friendly. After walking for a while, I was tired, and a battery car happened to pass by. There is no need to recruit. The driver will stop the car and ask us if we need a ride, which is very polite.
The check-out procedure is very convenient. The front desk manager also came to visit us and asked if we were staying well. He also escorted us personally. Before leaving, he found that his charger was left in the room, and he immediately drove the battery car without saying a word. I went to the villa to pick it up, and when I came back, I was sweating profusely. I believe he drove the car all the way and ran to pick it up for me. This kind of service is really attentive, and I really thank him!
This is the first time I have written a long story to praise a hotel, because Guilin Sunac Wanda Vista Hotel is trustworthy and worth experiencing. The service is meticulous and considerate, the staff are very amiable, and the food is delicious.
To my surprise, when I checked out and drove home by myself, someone from the hotel even called me to visit and asked if I had arrived home safely, which was really considerate. I will come again in the future.
